<TITLE>EX-99(1)</TITLE>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>EXHIBIT 99(1) </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g200152g0727070829122.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>HESS CORPORATION </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g200152g0727070829231.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:2.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>HESS REPORTS ESTIMATED RESULTS FOR THE SECOND QUARTER OF 2016 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Second Quarter Highlights: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Net loss was $392 million, or $1.29 per common share, compared with a net loss of $567 million, or $1.99 per common share, in the prior-year quarter </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Adjusted net loss was $335 million, or $1.10 per common share, compared to an adjusted net loss of $147 million, or $0.52 per common share, in the second quarter of last year </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>E&amp;P capital and exploratory expenditures were $485 million, down 52 percent from $1,006 million in the prior-year quarter </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Oil and gas production was 313,000&nbsp;barrels of oil equivalent per day (boepd); Bakken net production was 106,000 boepd </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Liza-2 well in the Stabroek block, offshore Guyana (Hess 30 percent) was successfully completed; confirms a world-class oil discovery with estimated gross recoverable resource for the Liza discovery of between 800
million and 1.4 billion barrels of oil equivalent </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Skipjack exploration well, offshore Guyana, which is a separate prospect 25 miles northwest of the Liza discovery, commenced drilling in July</I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Cash and cash equivalents were $3.1 billion at June 30, 2016; debt to capitalization ratio, excluding Bakken Midstream, was 23.5 percent </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2016 Revised Full Year Guidance: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>E&amp;P capital and exploratory expenditures are projected to be $2.1 billion </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B><I>&#149;</I></B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><I>Net production is forecast to be in the range of 315,000 to 325,000 boepd, excluding Libya </I></B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NEW YORK, July 27, 2016 &#151; </B>Hess Corporation (NYSE: HES) today reported a net loss of $392&nbsp;million, or $1.29 per common share, in the second
quarter of 2016 compared with a net loss of $567 million, or $1.99 per common share, in the second quarter of 2015.&nbsp;On an adjusted basis, the Corporation reported a net loss of $335 million, or $1.10 per common share, in the second quarter of
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
2016 compared with an adjusted net loss of $147 million, or $0.52 per common share, in the prior-year quarter.&nbsp;Lower production and realized selling prices reduced second quarter 2016
after-tax results by approximately $365 million compared to the second quarter of 2015.&nbsp;Operating costs, general and administrative expenses, and depreciation, depletion and amortization expense decreased compared with the prior-year quarter
due to lower production and ongoing cost reduction efforts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We remain confident in our ability to manage through the current
environment and deliver strong production and cash flow growth as oil prices recover,&#148; Chief Executive Officer John Hess said. &#147;During the quarter, we continued to pursue further cost reductions and now project our full-year 2016 E&amp;P
capital and exploratory expenditures to be about 48 percent below 2015 levels. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our resilient portfolio provides an attractive mix
of growth options including an unparalleled position in the Bakken, two significant offshore developments that will come online in 2017 and 2018, and the recent world-class oil discovery in Guyana.&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>(a)</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><I>Adjusted net income (loss) attributable to Hess Corporation excludes items affecting comparability summarized on page 6.&nbsp;A reconciliation of net income (loss) attributable to Hess Corporation to adjusted net
income (loss) attributable to Hess Corporation is provided on page 7. </I></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Exploration and Production: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Exploration and Production net loss in the second quarter of 2016 was $328 million compared to a net loss of $502 million in the prior-year
quarter.&nbsp;On an adjusted basis, the second quarter 2016 adjusted net loss was $271 million compared to $96 million in the prior-year quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Corporation&#146;s average realized crude oil selling price was $41.95 per barrel in the second quarter of 2016, down 25 percent from
$55.83 per barrel in the year-ago quarter, including the effect of hedging.&nbsp;The average realized natural gas liquids selling price in the second quarter of 2016 was $9.03 per barrel compared to $11.06 per barrel in the prior-year quarter while
the average realized natural gas selling price was $3.58&nbsp;per mcf, down from $4.49 per mcf in the second quarter of 2015. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net production in the second quarter of 2016 was 313,000&nbsp;boepd compared to pro forma net
production, which excludes assets sold, of 386,000 boepd in the second quarter of 2015.&nbsp;The decrease in production volumes resulted from unplanned downtime due to subsurface safety valve failures at the Tubular Bells Field and a mechanical
issue at one well in the Conger Field, both in the Gulf of Mexico, and planned facility downtime at several offshore fields including the Tubular Bells Field and the Valhall Field in Norway.&nbsp;In addition, volumes decreased in the Bakken shale
play and Equatorial Guinea due to lower investment levels, as well as the Malaysia/Thailand Joint Development Area primarily due to lower entitlement<B>, </B>which were partially offset by production growth from the Utica shale play. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the full year 2016, net production is projected to be 315,000 boepd to 325,000 boepd.&nbsp;The decline from our previous guidance of
330,000 boepd to 350,000 boepd primarily reflects unplanned downtime at two Gulf of Mexico fields.&nbsp;At the Tubular Bells Field two wells were shut-in for an extended period in the first half of 2016 due to defective subsurface safety
valves.&nbsp;The defective valves have been replaced.&nbsp;In July at the Tubular Bells Field, a subsurface safety valve in a third well failed and is expected to be remediated in the fourth quarter.&nbsp;Full year production is also impacted by a
mechanical issue at a well at the Conger Field, which is expected to be remediated in the fourth quarter.&nbsp;The full year impact of these temporary mechanical issues is expected to be approximately 20,000 boepd in 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Operational Highlights for the Second Quarter of 2016: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Bakken (Onshore U.S.):</I></B><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B>Net production from the Bakken was 106,000&nbsp;boepd compared to 119,000 boepd in the
prior-year quarter due to a reduced drilling program.&nbsp;The Corporation operated an average of three rigs in the quarter and brought 26&nbsp;gross operated wells on production.&nbsp;Drilling and completion costs averaged $4.8&nbsp;million per
operated well in the second quarter, down 14 percent from the year-ago quarter, while increasing our standard well design to a 50-stage completion from the previous 35-stage completion design. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Gulf of Mexico (Offshore U.S.):</I></B><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B>Net production from the Gulf of Mexico was 54,000 boepd compared to 84,000
boepd in the prior-year quarter primarily as a result of unplanned well downtime and extended planned shut-downs on third-party hosted production facilities at the Tubular Bells Field (Hess 57 percent) and the Conger Field (Hess 38
percent).&nbsp;Drilling and construction of production facilities at the Hess operated Stampede development project (Hess 25 percent) continued on schedule with first production targeted for 2018.&nbsp;Due to the current price environment and the
limited </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
time remaining on the leases, the Company chose not to pursue the project at the non-operated Sicily exploration prospect (Hess 25 percent) where hydrocarbons were encountered.&nbsp;Costs of both
wells drilled at Sicily were expensed in the quarter.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Valhall (Offshore Norway):</I></B><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B>Net production from the
Valhall Field (Hess 64 percent) averaged 19,000 boepd in the second quarter of 2016, down from 35,000 boepd in the year-ago quarter, as a result of a planned maintenance shutdown. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>North Malay Basin (Offshore): </I></B>Net production from the Early Production System in the North Malay Basin (Hess 50 percent)
averaged 6,000 boepd in the second quarter of 2016.&nbsp;Progress continues on Full Field Development with first gas projected in 2017.&nbsp;During the quarter, three wellhead platforms were installed and the Phase 1 development drilling campaign
remains on schedule with eight out of eleven planned wells now drilled. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Guyana (Offshore):</I></B><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B>On the
Stabroek Block (Hess 30 percent), the operator, Esso Exploration and Production Guyana Limited, completed drilling of the Liza #2 well.&nbsp;The well reached a total depth of 17,963 feet and encountered more than 190 feet of oil-bearing sandstone
reservoirs in Upper Cretaceous formations.&nbsp;The results confirm a world-class oil discovery with estimated gross recoverable resource for the Liza discovery of between 800 million and 1.4 billion barrels of oil equivalent.&nbsp;The operator is
currently drilling the Skipjack exploration well, which is a separate prospect 25 miles northwest of the Liza discovery. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Bakken Midstream: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Corporation&#146;s share of Bakken Midstream segment net income was $11 million in the second quarter of 2016 compared to $32 million in
the prior-year quarter, which primarily reflects the sale of a 50 percent interest in the Bakken Midstream segment on July 1, 2015. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Capital and
Exploratory Expenditures: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Exploration and Production capital and exploratory expenditures were $485 million in the second quarter of
2016 down 52 percent from $1,006 million in the prior-year quarter reflecting reduced activities in response to the weak commodity price environment.&nbsp;Bakken Midstream capital expenditures were $67 million compared to $65 million in the year-ago
quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Exploration and Production capital and exploratory expenditures are now projected to be approximately $2.1 billion for the full
year of 2016, down 48 percent from 2015, and $300 million </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
lower than our previous guidance.&nbsp;The reduced spending reflects certain deferred activity and the Corporation&#146;s continuing efforts to apply Lean principles to reduce costs and improve
operating efficiencies across our portfolio.&nbsp;Bakken Midstream capital expenditures for 2016 are estimated to be $290 million which is down from previous guidance of $340 million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Liquidity: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by
operating activities before changes in operating assets and liabilities was $257 million in the second quarter of 2016 compared to $729 million in the year-ago quarter.&nbsp;At June 30, 2016, the Corporation had cash and cash equivalents of
$3,095&nbsp;million and total debt, excluding the Bakken Midstream, of $5,868&nbsp;million.&nbsp;The Corporation&#146;s debt to capitalization ratio, excluding Bakken Midstream, was 23.5 percent at June 30, 2016. </P>

pre-tax) to write-off the Sicily #1 exploration well completed in 2015, based on the Company&#146;s decision in the second quarter of 2016 to exit the project.&nbsp;In addition, second quarter 2016 Exploration and Production results include an
after-tax charge of $22 million ($36 million pre-tax) associated with the termination of a drilling rig contract and an after-tax gain of $17 million ($27 million pre-tax) related to the sale of undeveloped acreage, onshore United States. </P>

charges totaling $21 million ($21 million pre-tax). </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Forward-looking Statements </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain statements in this release may constitute &#147;forward-looking statements&#148; within the meaning of Section 21E of the United States Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, and Section 27A of the United States Securities Act of 1933, as amended.&nbsp;Forward-looking statements are subject to known and unknown risks and uncertainties and other factors which may cause actual results to
differ materially from those expressed or implied by such statements, including, without limitation, uncertainties inherent in the measurement and interpretation of geological, geophysical and other technical data.&nbsp;Estimates and projections
contained in this release are based on the Company&#146;s current understanding and assessment based on reasonable assumptions.&nbsp;Actual results may differ materially from these estimates and projections due to certain risk factors discussed in
the Corporation&#146;s periodic filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission and other factors. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Non-GAAP financial measures </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Corporation has used non-GAAP financial measures in this earnings release.&nbsp;&#147;Adjusted net income (loss)&#148; presented in this release is defined
as reported net income (loss) attributable to Hess Corporation excluding items identified as affecting comparability of earnings between periods.&nbsp;&#147;Net cash provided by operating activities before changes in operating assets and
liabilities&#148; is defined as Cash provided by operating activities excluding changes in operating assets and liabilities.&nbsp;Management uses adjusted net income (loss) to evaluate the Corporation&#146;s operating performance and believes that
investors&#146; understanding of our performance is enhanced by disclosing this measure, which excludes certain items that management believes are not directly related to ongoing operations and are not indicative of future business trends and
operations.&nbsp;Management believes that net cash provided by operating activities before changes in operating assets and liabilities demonstrates the company&#146;s ability to internally fund capital expenditures, pay dividends and service
debt.&nbsp;These measures are not, and should not be viewed as, a substitute for U.S. GAAP net income (loss) or net cash provided by operating activities.&nbsp;A reconciliation of reported net income (loss) attributable to Hess Corporation (U.S.
GAAP) to adjusted net income (loss) as well as a reconciliation of net cash provided by (used in) operating activities (U.S. GAAP) to net cash provided by operating activities before changes in operating assets and liabilities are provided in the
release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Cautionary Note to Investors </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We use
certain terms in this release relating to resources other than proved reserves, such as unproved reserves or resources.&nbsp;Investors are urged to consider closely the oil and gas disclosures in Hess&#146; Form 10-K, File No. 1-1204, available from
Hess Corporation, 1185 Avenue of the&nbsp;Americas,&nbsp;New York, New York&nbsp;10036 c/o Corporate Secretary and on our website at www.hess.com.&nbsp;You can also obtain this form from the&nbsp;SEC&nbsp;on the EDGAR system. </P>
